sp008-002477_Yugavatara_06b	sahyAdriparvataSreRyA prItyA vikAsitezu hfdayakamalezu anyatamam etat kamalam svarAjyadevatAyAH padatale arpitam aBavat

sp008-002479_Yugavatara_06b	agrajaH samBAjiH api ParrAdaKAnasya sEnyam DUlisAt kftavAn iti
sp008-002480_Yugavatara_06b	itaHparam SahAjirAjasya vimocanamAtram avaSizwam AsIt
sp008-002481_Yugavatara_06b	putrayoH vizaye sTitaH pratIkAraBAvaH pitari Bavati cet
sp008-002482_Yugavatara_06b	SivarAjaH cintAmagnaH aBavat
sp008-002483_Yugavatara_06b	tanmaDye tasya budDibalam api kAryam akarot
sp008-002484_Yugavatara_06b	anukzaRam saH dehalIsTAya mogalacakravartine SahAjahAnAya ekam patram liKitavAn
sp008-002485_Yugavatara_06b	mama tIrTarUpI pitA aham ca BavataH siMhAsanasya sevAm kartum utsukO svaH
sp008-002486_Yugavatara_06b	BavataH anujYAm pratIkzamARaH asmi aham
sp008-002487_Yugavatara_06b	kintu bijApurasya rAjA kApawyena mama pitaram kArAgfhe sTApitavAn asti
sp008-002488_Yugavatara_06b	tasya vimocanAnantaram AvAm BavataH sevAyE upasTitO BavizyAvaH iti AsIt tasya patrasya ASayaH
sp008-002489_Yugavatara_06b	tadA SivarAjaH viMSativarzIyaH api nAsIt
sp008-002490_Yugavatara_06b	tasya rAjanItikuSalatA tAvat anupamA eva
sp008-002491_Yugavatara_06b	aPajalaKAnaH SahAjirAjam gajasya pfzWataH badDvA bijApurasya mArgezu SoBAyAtrAm kArayitvA
sp008-002492_Yugavatara_06b	kArAgfhe sTApitavAn AsIt Kalu
sp008-002493_Yugavatara_06b	itaHparam aham na jIvAmi iti SahAjirAjaH niScitavAn AsIt
sp008-002494_Yugavatara_06b	tAvati kAle dehalIsTAya cakravartine SivarAjaH guptarUpeRa patram liKitavAn asti
sp008-002495_Yugavatara_06b	iti vArtA kaTaYcit bijApuraSAsakasya karRapaTam AgatA
sp008-002496_Yugavatara_06b	bijApurasya ahaNkAram damayitum mahASUrO SahAjiSivarAjO SahAjahAnena yadi laByeyAtAm
sp008-002497_Yugavatara_06b	tarhi itoऽpyaDikA Ananda dAyinI vArtA kA anyA syAt tasya
sp008-002498_Yugavatara_06b	SahAjim uddiSya prayuktaH yamapASaH idAnIm bijApuraSAsakasya kaRWe Agatya patitaH AsIta
